91
Mr. Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
To Whom Do I Belong?
Among those gathered here, there are members from Japan, the United States, Europe, and various other countries. The members gathered here belong to different departments centered around the Unification Church. From this perspective, you can see that each of you has many boundaries centered around yourselves. If you take a step beyond, there are other departments and other countries, and we live in that position. 
Every human being wants to belong to an emotional subject or object.
Even when looking at Tarrytown, the land itself is divided among many owners. This land has passed through different ancestors and has a very complex history of ownership. When we look at it this way, we must ask whether it belongs to good people or bad people. Are we associated with good people or bad people?
Next, when you look at yourselves, you know that we have both body and mind. The question is whether our body and mind are completely united, allowing us to say we belong to someone, or whether our mind and body are in different positions. Ultimately, the issue is whether I belong to a better place centered around the Unification Church or a worse place.
When we look at the Unification Church itself, the question arises as to where it belongs among the countless religions centered around the absolute being known as God. The issue is whether we belong to God's external realm or internal realm.
From this perspective, what kind of place do you want to belong to? If God has money, do you want to belong to the money that God has? If God has knowledge, do you want to belong to God's knowledge? If God has emotion, do you want to belong to that emotion? Your answer would likely be that you want to belong to the emotion.
Why? Why do you want to belong to God's heart? Because God's heart is eternal. It can be a center, it can be a subject, but it cannot be relative. We must understand this here. When God makes a decision, it is not based on God's power, nor is it based on God's wisdom; it is based on God's heart that all decisions are made.
When you make a decision about something, what decides it is not wisdom but the heart. The heart decides whether it can be happy or good. The decisive factor in whether it can be good is whether it is connected to an emotional relationship or not, and we can see this in our daily lives.
Generally, we often hear friends asking what they like. What does that mean? It means whether that thing can bring joy to my heart. We must recognize that the word "joy" is always connected to an emotional state.
If you ask a man born as a man where he wants to belong, he will surely say, "I want to belong with a partner." If it is a woman, what will she belong to? Will she belong to material wealth, power, or knowledge? There is no woman who wants to belong to a man's knowledge. 
There is no woman who would say, "Ah, I want to belong to that man's power." So where would she want to belong? She would say she wants to belong to the heart. This is the same for everyone, regardless of gender. It is a common answer, isn't it? "Yes."
Among women, if there is one who says, "When I get married, I want to marry someone with money," that woman will become someone who belongs to money. If there is a woman who says, "I want to marry that man because he is a world-renowned scholar," that woman is lacking. Whether man or woman, where do they want to belong? Of course, they want to belong to a relative position, but to what aspect of the other do they want to belong? They want to belong to an emotional subject or object. This is a common answer in human history.
If there is a protagonist in this universe, and you ask where they want to belong, the answer would be the same. If God exists, wanting to belong to God's heart is the same. Even if there are many children centered around parents, the decisions made by those parents regarding their children, or the decisions made by the children comparing themselves to their parents, must ultimately be resolved based on the heart. We can find that everything is established by principles in our daily lives.
To become a person who loves the whole and can influence the whole
From this perspective, in front of God, there are many people belonging to the Unification Church. Furthermore, humanity is seen as belonging as well. So does God want to love only one person, or does He want to love everything centered around that person? The same applies here. Parents do not teach their children, "You should become a great person in our family, and forget about being a great person recognized by the citizens of the country." Parents wish for their children to be great not only in their family but also to be recognized as great by the sovereign of the nation.
Therefore, when they say, "At home, be good to your mother and father. In the neighborhood, do good deeds. At school, study hard. For the country, be patriotic," it all revolves around one point, passing through family and environment to influence the whole. We can glimpse that this is what is being said and taught in daily life. Why is that? Because if there is an absolute subject, everything is related to that subject. If there is a central being, it must be completely united without leaning in any direction, centered around the north, south, east, and west.
When you stand at the center, you must stand straight without being tilted to avoid distortion.
If you were to say to your parents, "I only like my mother and father, but I dislike other people," would God be pleased? Would your parents be pleased? If parents love their children, they would think, "I hope you love your siblings as well." This is the wish of parents. Furthermore, they educate their children to love not only their siblings but also the people of their neighborhood and country.
Why is that? When you love and establish emotional connections, that person will follow you as you move and will be governed by you. Ultimately, the wider the emotional connections around the parents centered on love, the broader the areas they can manage and govern. The entire environment exists by revering the grace of love centered around that love, which is the principle of existence in the world. Therefore, we must understand that we educate and wish for such a central being to be in a high position. Do you feel that way? "Yes."
The same goes for God. If you say, "Forget everything, I only want God. I only need God, nothing else," would God say, "Oh, you are so good. You are wonderful"? Would He say, "You little rascal, don't just love me; love the whole world with me"? What do you think? "He would say to love the whole world." You all know that. (Laughter)
To become a being belonging to God, you must stand in the same position as God.
Today's topic is about what I belong to and to whom I belong. What do you belong to, and to whom do you belong? "To God." So, do you belong to God? "Yes." Then, do you think just sitting quietly and saying, "I belong to God" will make God say, "Oh, really"? "No." This is where the problem lies.
So, does God belong to me, or do I belong to God? What is it? "Both." The fact that He belongs to me and I belong to Him is established only when we become completely one. Otherwise, I cannot say that I belong to God and that God belongs to me. Ultimately, we must become one with God. To do that, what must we do? We must be like God. Without standing in the same position as God, we cannot become one.
Now, look. If God wants to go to Korea, and you say, "Oh, forget Korea, stay in America," then no matter how much you claim to belong, you will be separated. What will happen then? Will you still belong to God? If you say, "Forget that, I don't need it," then you will be separated. Even if you claim to belong, you will be separated. At that point, the conclusion is that you cannot belong to God's side.
If you go further and say, "If God is like this, then God should not only be here in America but should also go to Africa," and if you say, "God, you stay here. I will go to Africa," knowing where God will go in the future, what will happen? After God saves America, will He have anywhere else to go? Surely, He will come to Africa. 
Then, do I belong to God, or does God belong to me? "God belongs to me." (Laughter) Since God followed me, He belongs to me. I am the subject. Will God come and say, "Hey, what have you done here?" If I have done something, He would say, "Hey, you did well. What else do you want to do?" This is how I become the subject.
Now, if we look at the Unification Church, there are many people interested in the teacher. I stopped by Washington yesterday, and since I had to come here today, I was about to leave when a female member asked me to stay a little longer. I said, "Oh, I am busy, and many members in New York are waiting for me. Should I stay in Washington?" and she insisted that I stay. Does that argument make sense? It does not. What does that mean? It means regarding the teacher…. Of course, that is nice. However, we must understand that a wise person is one who is concerned about the path the teacher must take. This principle applies in families, schools, societies, and any organization. We must recognize that this principle is the same. Isn't that right? "Yes."
If someone asks you where you belong, you would say, "Oh, I belong to the Unification Church." Where does the Unification Church belong? "To God." Furthermore, where does God belong? "To the heart." It belongs to the realm of heart. It is not just the heart; it belongs to the realm of heart. You must understand that it belongs to the realm of heart. Do you know what the realm of heart is? The realm of heart is not just a relationship between God and me. Before I belong to God, I belong to the whole and then belong to God. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."
Therefore, when you deal with the subject, do not just deal with this one aspect; deal with everything around you. When you deal with everything around you, you must connect in this way. (While writing on the board) When you love God, do you only love God's eyes? Do you only love this part? No. You must love everything around you. Do you like it when people who love each other hold hands and say, "Oh, I love you"? Do you like it when they hug each other? (Gesturing) What do you like? "Hugging." You must embrace and go around; you must go around. That is how love works.
In the same way, you must look around and create unity, wanting to love from a position where there is no disaster, even when reaching that center. This is the love that God desires.
Those who love God are those who love the world and love heaven and earth. Here is America. On the opposite side is Korea. Here is South America. There are many countries like this. (While writing on the board) When God says, "Hey, all you people! If there is someone who truly loves me, come out," who will come out? Everyone will want to come out. You too, right? "Yes."
When God calls for those who can love Him, they will run straight toward where God is. They will run in a straight line. So, when the first person arrives, will God say, "Hey, you came in first, so I know you love me"? Will He just watch? What do you think? Surely, He will say, "Hey, if you want to love me, I am greater than America, greater than Africa, and greater than anything in this world, so come and love me like that." He will ask, "Did you love America? Then did you love Africa? Did you love Asia?" At that point, everyone must say, "Yes, yes." "So, if you loved them all, then you can love me." This is theoretically correct. If you run with that love, even if you do not come in first, you can say, "I came in last because I loved like this."
What would you do if I said that? Forget about God for a moment; who would you choose as a partner in love? Is it the one who comes in first place, this one? If you give God's love to such a first-class person, they will steal love away. However, if you entrust love to someone like this (a last-place person), they will share it with all people. That's the truth. If that's the case for you, what about God? God is better than you, right? It's the same.

Do you want to receive God's love? "Yes." Do you want to become an eternal being belonging to God's love? "Yes." If that's the case, can you just say, "I only need God; I don't need anything else"? That won't work. It absolutely won't work. Just look at Christianity today. If you listen to the prayers, many people pray, "May our denomination do well, may our children do well..." Even though many people pray like that, Christianity is currently declining. When you look at such prayers, praying for my household is the biggest, and prayers for society are getting smaller and smaller. Prayers for the nation are also decreasing, and the number of people praying for the world is even fewer. And there are no prayers for God. Do you understand what I'm saying? "Yes."

But what do you think God thinks? God does not think about your household. God thinks about this world. God is thinking about the whole world. Before the God who thinks about the entire world, saying, "God, please take care of my family" does not work. It doesn't work. "God, our denomination, oh, our Presbyterian..." Such things are not even in God's consideration. "God, I must establish the world you desire. I must find a nation that can establish that world. I must find a church that can establish that nation. I must find individuals who can establish that church." Such prayers will work. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." We need to have such a perspective. Even when we pray, we should not pray in vain but pray in a way that God can directly hear. We need to pray from the standpoint of what God is thinking; if we pray in a way that does not align with God's heart, no matter how much we try, it won't work. Do you understand what I'm saying? "Yes."

So, what position does the Unification Church want to take before God? Is it a Unification Church that aims to make one family happy, a Unification Church that aims to make one nation happy, a Unification Church that aims to make the world happy, or a Unification Church that aims to make heaven and earth happy? Which one is it? This is the problem. "World." It's easy to say "world." (Laughter) This is a serious issue. God would say, "If you want to become my sons and daughters who belong to my heart, then you must connect with me from the position of caring for your family, your nation, the world, and heaven and earth." Would God say, "Forget all that and come directly to me"? What would you do?

Would you prefer to start from the family and go from there, or would you prefer to think of heaven and earth first, think of the nation God desires, think of the society God desires, think of the church God desires, think of the family God desires, and think of yourself as God desires? What path would you prefer? Think about it. "The second one." The answer is correct. God is such a being. That is why God is willing to sacrifice His most beloved servant, beloved sons and daughters, and beloved church to love this world.

Look at it. From the history of the Old Testament to the New Testament, the history of Christianity has sacrificed all the beloved people for the sake of the wicked people of the world; it has not blessed the beloved people. Isn't that right? "Yes." "Why would the teacher say such things from the beginning? How can I follow that? I want to be good, and the world should be good. I want to be good, and the nation should be good. I want to be good, and everything should be good." Isn't that how your hearts are? "No." Then, if you are to care for the world, when will you ever love your home and your parents? "Yes." If that's the case, isn't that unhappy? That is why opposing parents arise and take all of you from the Unification Church. Did the parents who took you away do well, or did you who got taken away do well? "We did." Why is that? It means you are on a higher level, a higher stage. You are transcending the various stages you need to go through. That is why you are better.

Your parents are supposed to follow the path you are going, not the other way around. You are on a higher dimension. That is why God concludes that a person who is loyal to another nation is more faithful than one who is loyal to their own nation. Do you understand? "Yes." That other nation could be the enemy's nation. Therefore, the logic of loving your enemies also comes from this standpoint.

If the Unification Church and the established church fight, which side would you choose? "Unification Church." (Laughter) From God's perspective, would He prefer you to stand with the Unification Church or with the established church? Think about it. If you side with the established church, what conclusion will arise? The established church members will see, "Wow, even though they are from the Unification Church, they are siding with us." Then they will submit to that person. They may have won with their fists and their blood, but in front of such a person, they have already lost in their hearts. They know they have lost. That is how God is.

So, what am I in the Unification Church? What kind of person am I standing here as Reverend Moon in the Unification Church? What am I? I am a leader, right? But should I teach you, "You should live only for the Unification Church, no matter what happens in the world"? Should I teach you, "You must sacrifice the Unification Church members for the sake of the world"? I teach that even if you fight among yourselves, you can still love the world when you go out. If you fight at home but can unite when you go out into the world, that person has hope. If you are a troublemaker at home but can be good when you go out into the world, that person has hope. Do you understand what I mean? The person who cannot do anything in the Unification Church but is capable in the world can succeed. Such a person will not perish. But no matter how well you do here, it won't work.

Who is closer, a member of the Unification Church or someone outside the Unification Church? Members of the Unification Church are closer, right? God will say, "As long as you love each other more than you love the people of the world, I will always accept you. I will always treat you well." Such a person can be accepted anywhere, anytime. If you are a citizen of the United States, if you love humanity more than you love American citizens, then such people will always be accepted. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Those who value the eternal spiritual world more than this world and strive for that nation and that world will always be accepted by God. It is the same principle. That is how God is; that is how God can be. Can God be if He only thinks of His own side?

Therefore, what is God doing? What kind of work is God doing? God is not doing His own work. He is not working for Himself. He is working for the world, for all people. You need to understand this. Do you understand what I'm saying? "Yes." God works for the world, so the world is needed.

Humanity is seeking such a God. Humanity must know that God is such a God. When humanity knows such a God and stands in a relative position to that God, humanity will be liberated. In this light, do you also want to receive God's love? "Yes." Then what should you do? Should you become someone who runs straight like I mentioned earlier, or should you become someone who goes around? "Someone who goes around." (Laughter)

So you need such a church, such a nation, such a family, and such individuals. You need individuals with such thoughts, families with such thoughts, nations with such thoughts, and a world with such thoughts. Individuals with such thoughts will not live for themselves, no matter how well they live together; they will live for the world. If there is such a family, even if they are told to live only for their family, they will not live for themselves but for the world. If there are such nations, churches, and peoples, they will not live for their own nation, church, or country but for the world. If there is a church that teaches such content, that church is the true church that God desires. Do you understand? "Yes."

What kind of nation is a true nation? It is a nation that lives centered on such official principles for the world. This applies to all individuals, families, societies, churches, and nations that embrace such societies and churches. If they live with such a perspective and move with such a perspective, that nation is a true nation. Do you understand what a true nation is? "Yes." That is a true nation.

Then what is a true heaven on earth? A true heaven on earth is not living for this land but living for the true God and the true heavenly kingdom. It is the same. Do you understand what I'm saying? "Yes." If you were to draw this, there would be a point at the top, and this is the family, this is society, this is the tribe... This would be the picture. Such individuals are protected by heaven and earth. Such individuals are protected by the nation. (Drawing on the board) Such individuals are protected by society. Such individuals are protected by the family. Do you understand what it means to be protected? "Yes." If such a person exists, not only will the church protect them, but the nation will protect them, and the world will protect them. How wonderful is that? With just one person, the family protects them, society protects them, the church protects them, the nation protects them, and the world protects them, and even God protects them. How safe is that? That position is a happy position that cannot be harmed no matter how much damage is done. Even if I am alone somewhere, such a world, such a family, and such a heart will embrace me. Do you understand what I'm saying? "Yes."

Let us become people who can be protected by the fence of heart and the fence of love. The teacher may not have such qualifications, but when I go to Korea, do you care about Korea or do you care about America? "Oh, the teacher is in Korea." And when I go to England, the Unification Church members say, "The teacher is in England." Their hearts are all like that. That is what it means. Is that a miserable person? "No." If such a person exists, even when dealing with individuals, they elevate them as high as the heavens, and even when individuals deal with that person, they represent the value of protecting them from the perspective of the whole...

This is how the fence becomes a fence of heart and a fence of love. It means that such a fence protects me in layers. If you think, "I am number one," and try to live for yourself, how pitiful that is. Everything will disappear. That becomes a hose through which Satan can come and go at any time. So, would you rather be a person whose fence of love protects you in layers, or a person through whom Satan can come and go freely? "Number one." Being number one is not easy. It's not easy, which is why it's difficult. Even God finds it hard. It is something God has been doing until now.

Let us be members of the Unification Church who do such work. Let our church become such a Unification Church. Do you like this Unification Church? "Yes." I personally do not really like the Unification Church. When I think of my difficult path... (Laughter) It's true. It's an honest statement. If it weren't for God, I couldn't do this, I wouldn't do it. Because God is here, and because God knows such things, I have lived my whole life...

Look at me. Throughout my life, I have been persecuted, I have been pointed at, and it has been a problem wherever I go. Have I done anything bad since I came to America? Honestly, let's be honest. Am I doing things that deserve criticism or things that deserve praise? It's the opposite. I have done good things. I have corrected the minds of those who use drugs, those hippie-like people, to make them useful for the nation, for the world, and for their parents, and that is why there is this uproar. And for about three years, I have spent tens of millions of dollars in America. While everyone else comes to America to take everything, Reverend Moon comes with money and spends it in America to save American youth. Is that a bad thing?

Korea and Japan may be poorer than America, but they are doing things to help the Americans who are living well by making them suffer more. Isn't that what is happening? Have you seen anyone who says they like God? Do you all like God now? "Yes." Everyone only says "God" when things go well for them; if things don't go well, they say, "God is irrelevant." That's how everyone is.
If you go out with God's will, you are destined to suffer and be persecuted throughout your life. You are only doing the things you dislike the most, and since you are being taught that way, the parents who take their sons and daughters away and educate them like that will inevitably oppose it. They will not praise it. Therefore, I do not like the Unification Church, to be honest. From a human perspective, I cannot like the Unification Church. (Laughter) It’s the truth. Isn’t that the case for you too? “No.” But if I were alone, it would be different, but since God is here, it cannot be. That doesn’t mean I wish God didn’t exist. Instead, I want to monopolize the love that exists within God. Why? Because it is the most precious thing. I know that it is the most precious thing. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.”

This Reverend Moon you are looking at is nothing, but God loves him. It seems to me that God loves me. How can I know that? Because when I do things that no one else can do, I know that I am being helped in those adventurous endeavors. When I go to prison and am hungry, someone brings me food. When I become weary and collapse as a wanderer, I am led to a house that can comfort me and given food. When I travel a long way and the path seems endless, God worries and buys me a ticket. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.” 

Reverend Moon, this little person, is being cared for by God transcending space, and how glorious is that? It didn’t happen just because I made a phone call. Do you understand? It is God who can do that. Look again. When I came to America, all the Americans opposed me saying, “Reverend Moon, go bankrupt. Die, die.” But did I die? “No.” As time goes by, I became more famous. In three to four years, the whole of America came to know me. Isn’t that right? (Applause) 

If you look closely, Reverend Moon does not seem like he will fail. Whether white, black, or yellow, when Reverend Moon says “Let’s do it,” everyone says “Let’s do it!” It doesn’t seem like he will fail. Do you think this organization will fail or prosper? What do you think? “It will prosper.” I believe that if God exists, He cannot let it fail. Why? Because I am putting in so much effort and trying to save all humanity in any way I can. But if I work hard and die, would God say, “Now that Reverend Moon is dead, it’s good and easy. When Reverend Moon was alive, he was so busy trying to save the world, and I was troubled, but now that you are dead, I can rest”? “No.” What would God do? The more He loves, the more He would say, “I know the regret of not achieving what you wished for in your lifetime, so even if you are gone, I will fulfill it for you.” That is God. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.” Therefore, the Unification Church cannot fail. It cannot fail.

You will add to the Unification Church, not diminish it, right? “Yes.” Even those who are dozing off will add to it? “Yes.” (Laughter) If you are sleepy, why did you come here? Should you be sitting here dozing off? You could go and sleep comfortably. “The teacher is coming to speak, so I’ll take a bath and sleep. Why are you all sitting here dozing off?” (Laughter) Sitting on the cold concrete floor without a chair and dozing off, and yet, you don’t even know when you fell asleep…. (Laughter) Should I feel sympathy for that or not? “You should feel sympathy.” (Laughter) It’s something you enjoy doing…. “No, it’s not.”

The way to receive God's love is to sacrifice more broadly and further. 

Since a lot of time has passed, let’s conclude. You belong to God. Where do you belong to God? You belong to God’s heart. Then you must have surely understood how to belong to God's heart. Did you not know? Because of that, Unification Church members should always put a world map on the wall and look at the world. 

When you see through God’s eyes, where will you look? Will you look at the well-fed and well-off America, or will you look at India, where people are starving to death? God looks at India. Will you look at the college students in America who have nothing to do and are streaking, or will you look at the children in the remote areas of Africa, living like savages, unable to attend school and living naked? God does not look at America; He looks at the poor Africa. 

If there is someone who would scrape everything from wealthy America and give it to Africa, God will think of that person. He will love that person. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.” Therefore, our Unification Church should earn money in America and build great universities in Africa, and establish great universities across the five oceans and six continents. Is that good or bad? “It is good.” Even if the Americans who oppose the Unification Church dislike it? “Yes.” (To a girl whose voice is particularly loud) You are very noisy. (Laughter) The way of thinking is different.

The teacher thinks that those who study well and have excellent grades in America should not just become excellent American citizens but should go out into Africa or the world and become true saints. Do you understand? “Yes.” The more developed a country’s citizens are, the more they should be sent abroad. They should be sent abroad to pioneer. The teacher thinks that way. Is that a wrong thought or a good thought? “It is a good thought.” If that day comes, think about how the world will be. The only way to save the world is that way. There is no other way to save the world. You cannot save the world. By doing so, will God see and say, “You are doing well,” or will He say, “Hey, you guys are doing it wrong”? “He will say you are doing well.” Now you understand.

The way to receive God's love is through broader and further sacrifice. The more one tries to bestow grace with their own hands, the more they become a person belonging to God's heart, and that goes without saying. Therefore, our Unification Church members must do missionary work in at least three countries. Why must it be so? Because Adam had three sons, and Noah had three sons. Also, Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob are three generations; the restoration era must also pass through the first Adam, the second Adam, and the third Adam, going through three stages. That is why it must be the same for countries. You must go through three countries. You must understand that you cannot go to heaven without passing through three countries.

Even looking at the teacher, you must go through Japan, then America, and then the Soviet Union. (Applause) That is the path the teacher must take. We must also save the communist world. Are we going to just cut and kill all communists? The democratic world must unite and stand before heaven’s will to save the communist world. Then, which country’s people should be sent to Moscow? Would it be easier for an American or an African? “An American.” Right. Since it is easier for an American, an American must do it. Just as I did here, you must also go to the Soviet Union and do it.

You all must understand that you cannot go to heaven without passing through three countries. You cannot go to heaven by dying in your own country. You must understand that only those who have passed through three countries can receive God's love. Do you understand what I mean?

To serve humanity and make achievements for heaven, what must you do to belong to God’s heart? You must not think that you are working for yourself when you are doing your work; you must always think that you are working for the world. You must implant the idea that you are working for heaven and earth. You must hold it strongly. Because I am for the world…. If we divide the world’s races, there are white, black, and yellow…. Five colors of races, right? You must think that the five colors of races are working together. Do you understand what I mean? You must discover yourselves as those who truly love like brothers and work for humanity with one heart in the position of God.

You are doing business to be filial to your parents, to be loyal to your country, to do good for humanity, and to do it for God, so you should be dignified. You should be dignified in evangelism. There is nothing to be ashamed of. It is different. Even if I make you do fundraising and sell peanuts, you should think of it as dignified. There is nothing to be ashamed of. You are doing better than making a Ford car factory and selling cars.
Our Unification Church members believe that the love for a higher purpose, such as love for the nation, love for parents, and love for heaven, grows larger rather than smaller. That is why the Unification Church is developing day by day. If we do not develop every day, then heaven and everything else, including Reverend Moon's words, are all fake. It's a lie.

Why do we develop? Movements centered around such love are bound to hold onto everything. Therefore, it is destined to develop. The teacher knows this, which is why he sometimes talks to the members in Korea all night, even if they are tired and exhausted. What do I always worry about? When anyone comes to talk here in Korea or Japan, what do they all think when it becomes one o'clock or two o'clock? They think, “Oh, I wish I could sleep. It would be nice if I could be sent home!” That's right. But a parent's heart is different, a parent's heart. Isn't that how God is? The one who loves…

That is why they always want to follow and feel that they are being watched with interest. How beautiful is that world of affection (情)?

Now, you should understand. So, do not speak words that are not in your heart. Absolutely do not. It will catch you. It will catch you in the heavenly law. And do not act like that. Do you understand now? “Yes.” Since there is value in this content, can you not speak and act well? 

The reason we need to evangelize
Why do we need to evangelize? If we evangelize a person who has a good character and comes from a lineage that has cultivated a good foundation, when that one person is evangelized, because they were evangelized through me, they can go to a place better than the house or environment they would have in the spirit world. You need to understand that. Do you know what I mean? “Yes.” Since we do not know who such a person is, the more we evangelize, the more we rise to a position that is above the environment where many people can live. Also, when God blesses, if they were evangelized through me, He gives the blessing through me. You need to know that. Moreover, in the Unification Church, we have even given the names of sons and daughters of faith, spiritual sons and daughters.

Imagine the person who can receive the greatest blessings in the spirit world standing in a position like my grandchildren. When you go to the spirit world, you will go to a place beyond that position of blessing. Even if you may not look good and have nothing, because I know all these secretive contents, I can receive blessings more than anyone in the world. You need to understand that this privilege exists in this position, which no king, empress, or queen could have.

Can President Carter's mother live in the White House? “Yes.” Does the mother have the qualifications of a president? No. She does not have the qualifications to live together. But because she is the president's mother. 

If a son who has been evangelized goes to live in God's palace, can I go live there? “Yes.” It’s the same principle. It’s fine to become a king or whatever. A path of greater secrets will open. You need to know that there is a privilege here to carry and control the eternal world’s secret tradition.

And by just a few days of effort in evangelizing, can we not bring up hundreds of thousands of educated people who spent millions of dollars? So, someone who can be more loyal to me than anyone else and absolutely obey my commands can emerge, but you don’t do it? So, it’s cheap. The children that parents have painstakingly raised are all taken away by you members of the Unification Church, so it is natural for them to oppose you. It is understandable. While you say that there is great value in doing this here, their parents are trying to reap value from their children, but they are gone, so the parents have no choice but to oppose.

And you need to know how many miracles are happening for you. Just listening to the Unification Church principles for one week, people who have been living freely until now all stop and fight for this purpose, for God. When you think about how revolutionary and miraculous this is, it is amazing. It is astonishing to think that I am prepared to do such things. You should feel that way. “Yes.”

Whether they are black, yellow, or white, they need to feel that. They should feel like an earthquake or an explosion. When you think that what God could not do for 6,000 years, I can do in a week, in a few days, or in a few hours, how wonderful is that? (Applause) That’s right. Think about it. How exciting is this? Can this mouth rest? Can this mouth be quiet? It should keep talking all night. How can it stay still, wanting to move around? Can this mouth, these feet stay still? Imagine if you evangelized a thousand people before you die. If you evangelized a thousand people on earth, it would take three years to meet them all, three years. It takes three years. When you understand this meaning, how grateful would you be when the person who evangelized you comes? Think about it.

Just finding those sons and daughters… Would you neglect someone who comes once a year or once every three years? In the future, in 10 or 20 years, such times will come. You will all be able to search for your sons and daughters, your spiritual sons and daughters, across borders, and what will you do if you have not evangelized at all? Look. You can give far and wide to well-known and great people, and if you have heaven and earth, you can have it broadly, but if you have nothing, you have to be alone. You have to be alone. 

People need education, and then they need to have their sons and daughters. More important than education is having sons and daughters. So, should we evangelize or not? We should, right? “Yes.” If you have such sons and daughters, you should talk to them until your mouth wears out and work until your hands wear out… That is what you should do as a human before God, and it is what you can boast of before God. There is nothing else.

I must build my own heaven
What glory would there be in speaking and acting for myself? Do you understand? Will you do that from now on? “Yes.” Never speak for free. Am I speaking a lot with the heart of heaven, humanity, and the heart of the world, or am I speaking a lot for my family’s private life? You should always compare what you do more. Do not engage in idle chatter, idle talk. The same goes for actions. Going for others, for evangelism, for public work can always remain, but if done unnecessarily…

From today, I will tally how much you speak and act unnecessarily. You should compare and cut it out. Whether you are evangelizing or going out to fundraise, you must always do it with a heart. Sleep with a heart, wake up with a heart, eat with a heart, and act with a heart. You must always live that way.

Even if you earn money like that, it will work; otherwise, God will not remember. The same goes for actions. You do it voluntarily; no one is forcing you. Isn’t that right? Studying is the same. Does the teacher do everything for you? Your heaven must be built by you. Do you understand? “Yes.” Let’s see a show of hands from those who will live like that from now on. Put your hands down. (Applause) 

Questions and Answers with Reverend Sun Myung Moon
Q: People within the Unification Church have heard Reverend Moon's words a lot, but ordinary people outside have not heard Reverend Moon's words regarding the issues that are the subject of debate at all. I think it is very important to hear Reverend Moon's words directly. Even if the truth is spoken, those in opposition can interpret it differently, and while the church speaks the truth, the content can be completely changed and conveyed in a way that fosters disbelief among outsiders. Because of that, I have often quoted the words of believers and non-believers. I hope that this will become another value of this book. This book will help people talk and interpret in the right way.

That’s right. Your story is true. I am very pleased that scholars like you are treating our movement and our criticisms equally and are evaluating them objectively and fairly. Most of the misunderstandings about our movement in America stem from a lack of understanding of us. 

So, I will gladly answer your questions. As you know, I have dedicated my life, honor, my entire family, and everything to the Unification Church movement. If I did not have absolute certainty that this is right, I would not be doing this. There is a true meaning in this, so those who follow me will not be at a loss. I do not act out of temporary feelings or arbitrarily.

The Unification Church movement has a deep spiritual origin. It has appeared in this era by God's command. I am being guided by God. Many people think that I am doing everything my way, but that is not the case.

In some ways, I am somewhat grateful for the negative reputation in the world or the negative interpretations by Americans. This proves that the revelations I receive are new. All religious founders, including Jesus, were persecuted by the people of their time. Likewise, when the time comes, people today will understand me, and there will be a dramatic conversion like that of the Apostle Paul. I knew from the beginning that I would face trials and tribulations when I came to America. However, such trials and persecutions only make our members and me stronger. A true religious movement flourishes and develops through suffering.

Q: You believe that God chose Korea to play a special role in the development of religion today. Please explain in detail why you think Korea was chosen for God's purpose.

Korea has unique characteristics in several ways. First, the Korean people are a homogeneous race. Second, Koreans are very religious. They have an innate understanding of religion. Third, they understand suffering. Koreans have had to endure endless trials and difficulties throughout history. In such conditions, Koreans have developed an immortal spiritual expectation with a spirit of loyalty and dedication.

All of these are the most important characteristics that a people chosen by God must possess. This is because it aligns with God's nature. No one has suffered as much as God in the historical process. The reason is that God's children have separated from Him. Since the fall of humanity, God has been continuously working for the blessing of His children.

Humans do not understand God's aching heart. To truly understand God's suffering and communicate with Him, the three characteristics mentioned above are very important. The chosen people of Israel 2,000 years ago also possessed these characteristics. Today, Korea has many commonalities with God's heart. Because of the experiences of suffering and sorrow they have endured, Koreans can easily understand God's sorrow and aching heart. That is why they can easily respond to God's call.

In this regard, we can also find an answer to why God chose me as the mission bearer of His providence in this era. There is the same reason here. I possess an unwavering will because I am deeply religious. And I have been tempered by numerous trials and hardships. When God wanted to reveal the providential will and entrust me with that mission, I could easily understand His heart. I wept knowing that situation. At that time, I resolved to devote my entire life to comforting God's aching heart. Since then, it has become my glory and privilege to bear God's suffering on my shoulders. The goal of all my actions has become to liberate God from sorrow.

Q: Please tell us a few words about the religious situation in Korea when Reverend Moon began to understand God's will and work.

As the birthplace of a new spiritual movement, Korea had a very appropriate background in 1945. At that time, Christianity was flourishing in Korea. The depth of faith among Christians was tremendous. There were also many spiritual groups that had received revelations that a new spiritual movement would begin. They were groups entrusted with the mission of John the Baptist. However, these groups could not testify to the new spiritual movement.

Accepting a new spiritual movement always comes with human responsibility. Even 2,000 years ago, the Jews lacked the humble attitude necessary to accept Jesus. Their inability to accept Him stemmed from their ignorance of the shared responsibility of humanity. Even to this day, established churches reject our new spiritual movement. That is why I had to start with the role of John the Baptist, which serves as my internal expectation to fulfill my mission.

Q: From the perspective of traditional Christian theology, the Unification Principle can be considered heretical. However, there is something new in the Unification Church. I am curious about what Reverend Moon would say about the role of God's new revelation before evaluating it. Does it mean a departure from traditional Christian theology?

First, Christianity has significantly deviated from God's fundamental purpose and providence over its 2,000-year history. For 2,000 years, Christianity has split into hundreds of denominations. This is due to factionalism. Because Christians build walls among themselves, they hinder their own paths. This is the most important reason why God needs humans with a new sense of purpose.

God is preparing a new vision of life that will permeate the hearts of humans. However, if there is no object that approaches in a new and fresh way, God cannot show the way to fulfill His original purpose of creation. The Unification Principle is that new revelation.

Those who participate in the Unification Church movement not only find a new vision but also gain the power of the new Holy Spirit. Such people become the mainstay of a new revolution to establish the eternal kingdom of God.
The second important thing is that our movement takes the salvation of the world as its primary goal. Our personal salvation is a secondary issue. We are willing to sacrifice ourselves for the world and humanity. In contrast, many Christians are more concerned with securing their own place in heaven and obtaining eternal life before others.

In fact, the teaching of sacrifice is not new. It is fundamentally based on the teachings of Jesus Christ. Jesus came to save this world, not to save Himself. Nevertheless, Christianity has lost the fundamental spirit of Jesus and has distorted His purpose. I have come simply to renew the spirit of Jesus Christ. His ideals have become dim over a long history. We are now revitalizing and bringing them to life.

I always teach that the Unification Church itself is not the goal. I must serve as a tool of God to save the world. This is the reason for the existence of the Unification Church.

There are already enough churches in the world, but this world still needs salvation. The Unification Church is very proactive in God's work from this standpoint. We take risks to eliminate sin where it exists. We do not flee from sin; we fight against it. An example of this can be seen in the Watergate incident. At that time, the wise thing for me to do would have been to pretend not to know. Being involved in this matter would lead to a bad reputation. However, I did not shy away from that situation and issued a statement regarding my involvement. This is because I know that religious leaders must speak about the current pressing issues and strive to find solutions.

This also answers the question of "Why does the Unification Church engage in many issues that others do not understand?" Our perspective is on a different dimension than that of the people of the world. We do not take predetermined actions day by day; rather, we view everything from a global and long-term perspective. We act for the well-being of nations, the world, and our descendants. In order to achieve certain goals for future humanity, even if it leads to a bad reputation and clear losses in the present, we carry it out. We suffer greatly because of this, yet we continue to do such work. It is an adventure and a very dangerous endeavor. Even if our activities may sometimes seem foolish in the eyes of others, if they are right from God's standpoint, we move forward together for that purpose.

Q: Pastor Moon, you live in the midst of the secular world, and that has become a subject of controversy. In attempting to lead the world toward God in the midst of the secular, is there not a risk that you may fall into the confusion of the secular world yourself?

This is a religious movement. We do everything with religious conviction. Therefore, instead of becoming victims of the situation or taking on the situation, we must become victors even at a cost. The Unification Church under my leadership sometimes takes on tasks that are closer to the impossible than to the ordinary. However, we never abandon a task in its unfinished stage or leave it incomplete. I want to gain a reputation that once the Unification Church moves, it will surely accomplish and achieve its goals.

Q: Each of Pastor Moon's tours of cities and states, as well as the 'Madison Square Garden rally,' 'Yankee Stadium event,' and 'Washington Monument event,' must have their significance. However, they are not understood at all by the outside world. Could you share your views on the importance of these events?

I came to America to proclaim a new era and new truth. Whether people accept me soon or not, it is my duty bestowed by God to proclaim it. God appeared to me and commanded me to go to America and convey the truth. I hesitated because I do not speak English, but God still commanded me to go. Through my speaking tours, I have somewhat fulfilled this mission of proclamation. During the 'Day of Hope Great Feast,' I toured all 50 states. It was not just a typical evangelistic meeting. It has great significance in terms of God's providence and the spiritual aspect.

I do not know how much you perceive and understand the spiritual world, but that world is very vivid in the Unification Church movement. The Unification Church movement is not only a horizontal movement but also a vertical movement with God. Everything we do is reflected in the spiritual world, and we reflect the spiritual world as well, and the collaboration of these two worlds is a characteristic of our movement.

From a horizontal perspective, our activities may seem meaningless. Sometimes they may appear to waste time, resources, and energy. However, sometimes what we do on the ground helps the spiritual world. We also work to create conditions for the Holy Spirit to overflow on this earth.

The established churches and religious organizations in America are generally leaning towards a secular mindset and are contaminated by secular culture, leading to decline. However, the Unification Church is different. We do not feel any spiritual regression within the Unification Church movement. We are pioneers, and our will is like a volcano.

You may have heard me say in various speeches after the 'Washington Monument event' that now is the time when the spiritual world is ready to cooperate. The spiritual world is prepared to collaborate with our movement. As you know, I declared October 4, 1976, as 'Cheon Seung Il' (Heavenly Victory Day) after the 'Washington Monument event.' This marked the dawn of a new era, and in the spiritual world, the barriers between religions have effectively collapsed. In reality, spirits are cooperating with the earthly world. This phenomenon is occurring in various forms.

Q: What do you think is your role in relation to the role of Jesus?

One of the most important revelations I have received is that Jesus Christ did not come to die. He came to fulfill the responsibility of the Savior given by God to establish heaven on earth. However, by being crucified, Jesus offered Himself as a sacrifice to this world of disbelief and achieved only spiritual salvation through His resurrection. This is the teaching of the Unification Principle.

The complete salvation that encompasses both spirit and body was God's ultimate purpose and planned goal for humanity during the time of Jesus. That mission was not fully accomplished. However, we must realize that this was not a fault on the part of Jesus Christ. It was the result of the people of that time rejecting Jesus, who came as the Messiah. There is much misunderstanding about this point today.

The prophecy of the Second Coming exists because God's original purpose was not fully realized the first time. Therefore, in order to fully fulfill God's will, a reform movement led by the Messiah must begin on earth. The Unification Church movement and my mission are to proclaim that the era of the Messiah has come again.

From the perspective of the established church, this new revelation of mine will appear not only special but also revolutionary.

I understand why established Christians call us a heresy. However, the most important thing is who God calls a heretic. From God's standpoint, my teachings are thoroughly orthodox. If the mission of Jesus Christ had been fully accomplished in that era, there would be no reason for the Unification Church to appear. Therefore, my mission would not have been necessary.

Q: I understand that the goal of the Unification Church is to unify all churches and form one large family. Nevertheless, Pastor Moon's movement is causing family breakdowns in Korea and here in America, leading to tensions and opposition from other religions. Do you consider this to be ironic? How do you intend to work towards achieving your goals?

That is certainly ironic. However, from a spiritual perspective, great blessings will be bestowed upon the families of the sons and daughters working for this new mission of the Unification Church. Moreover, this is an emergency on a global scale to establish heaven. When an emergency occurs in a nation, a soldier temporarily leaves his wife and children behind to protect his country. From God's perspective, these sons and daughters have been called for the greatest emergency to establish heaven and for the glorious mission of establishing heaven. People complain so much because they cannot see the spiritual aspect.

I have not separated or destroyed families. In fact, in many cases, I have restored families and united them in happiness. I have received countless letters of gratitude from parents who are happy because of this.

The reason people become involved in the Unification Church movement is not due to their age but because of the magnetic attraction of the truth contained within the Unification Principle. When they encounter the truth, anyone is bound to ignite. When one comes into contact with the most absolute and perfect truth, they cannot remain attached to the lower truths they have believed until now.

The relationship between parents and children is filled with love and beauty. Nevertheless, if a child experiences greater love than what they have received from their parents at home, they may think they need to seek a greater love for spiritual satisfaction. When people discover this life force, they cannot help but be drawn to that attraction. God's new word is the foundation of life and light.

Jesus Christ is the 'Prince of Peace' and came to bring true peace. However, He said, 'Do not think that I came to bring peace to the world; I did not come to bring peace but a sword.' Does this contradict His title as the 'Prince of Peace'? No. We must understand that He came for true and eternal peace. This is because a fundamental transformation of human life is inevitable to establish eternal peace.

To reach this true peace, Jesus first sought to bring about transformation in human life. In that sense, He came to fight. He aimed to fundamentally transform individuals, society, nations, and the world. Because of this, He faced all kinds of opposition when He taught. When truly establishing a new society, many obstacles follow. Thus, Jesus suffered and was ultimately crucified.

Today's world requires bold transformation to establish a God-centered world. I have come to achieve this transformation. The Unification Principle influences human life and ignites the Holy Spirit in hundreds of thousands. Therefore, this truth will soon be revealed as true, and families scattered across the world will be unified. Nevertheless, we face tensions and opposition. However, if we reflect on the lessons of history, we can understand that such persecution is normal and inevitable during the pioneering phase of a serious spiritual movement.

In the early days in Korea, many housewives came to the Unification Church. Initially, it seemed that more women were attracted to the truth. Women are thought to be more religious than men. However, they faced terrible persecution at home. Many husbands hated that their wives were going to church and used all kinds of methods to prevent it. Sometimes they even cut their wives' hair. This was because women would be too embarrassed to go outside if their hair was cut. Still, they came to church at midnight to pray and worship. They wrapped their heads in scarves and still came to church. Sometimes the scarves would blow away in the wind, but they did not care at all. For them, coming to church was better than being embarrassed. Some had all their clothes taken away but still came to church in rags.

The power that leads people to the source of life is astonishingly strong and hard to believe. The Unification Church faced unfair persecution in its early days precisely because of this.

Seeing this, people assume that Pastor Moon must be giving people some kind of stimulant or drug to brainwash them. Such persecution has occurred not only in America but also in Korea.

Q: As you know, Pastor Moon, the training and evangelistic methods of the Unification Church have sparked much controversy. I would like to know if you see any fundamental differences in the way you train and evangelize people compared to other forms of evangelism.

As you would know if you visited many of the regional headquarters of the Unification Church, what we are doing is a process of education. We tell people about the 'Principle' and invite them to come and listen. Everything we do is about teaching the 'Principle.' We hold workshops, but what is training? It is simply teaching the 'Principle.' Moreover, all doors are open, and anyone can leave our church at any time. However, people choose to stay to hear the teachings. The methods of evangelism and witnessing are fundamentally not new. They are no different from those of regular churches. The only difference is the teaching of the truth we possess, which is the 'Principle.'

Another point I want to mention is regarding the many people's thoughts that when American youth come to me, I must be hypnotizing them. In reality, I have never directly shared the Principle with anyone who is newly entering. They do not come to meet me until they become part of the family. They sometimes come to church on Sundays to hear my talks, but that is all. Whether I am here or not does not affect the Unification Church's gaining or losing members. There is the truth of the 'Principle,' and anyone can hear and teach that message. The 'Principle' helps people realize a deeper understanding of God's will and a more direct relationship with God.

Many members engaged in economic activities have hardly ever met me. They listen to the teachings of the 'Principle' and become core members devoted to this purpose. They do not do this because of my personal influence or because I told them they would be cursed if they did not do it. Many people in the world seem to think that I have attached high-performance devices to the members engaged in economic activities and control them. That does not make any sense.

Q: It seems that people in the world are trying to detect any conspiracy behind the Unification Church and its activities. Why do such suspicions arise?

You know well that the Unification Church does not have any secrets. However, many people think we are surrounded by secrecy, like operations conducted by the CIA. Our activities are completely open, so it is a remarkable irony. I have nothing to hide. People do not come to our church to verify the facts directly. We always keep our doors open and welcome them. If they were to come and investigate, why would we be known as a place of conspiracy? 

In reality, it is those who feel intimidated by me and the Unification Church, that is, those who oppose us, who spread such rumors.
it has been revealed. Established churches are fearful. They are anxious that their churches, land, and buildings might be handed over to us. In particular, they are very defensive because they fear losing their young people as many of them become members of the Unification Church. The only way they can protect themselves is, as has happened throughout history, to portray their adversaries in the worst light and to depict our doctrines and methods in the most negative way.

However, I and our church have faced numerous criticisms and persecutions over the past 30 years, but ultimately we have overcome them and have been able to lay a successful foundation today. This has happened because God has cooperated behind the scenes. I sincerely thank God who has led us to victory.

Today, many people feel threatened by me, and they think they must expel me by any means necessary. This is because they believe I will take away their prosperity, future, and even their children. However, I harbor no malice towards those who strive to destroy me. The mission that God has given me is to liberate them from hatred and fear and to guide them to eternal salvation as a light. We wish to unite with them under God's blessing.

Question: The management of assets and money by Reverend Moon is the biggest point of contention regarding the Unification Church. Why do you believe the management and use of assets is necessary for the church's programs, and what is your view on asset management?

The properties we own in New York and around the world are part of God's blessings. All material things are gifts created by God to be given to children. However, due to human fall, we have not been able to become true sons and daughters of God. But there will come a time when they will return to God's lineage and be able to govern all creation as direct heirs, using it for God's glory.

I do not view material as inherently evil. It is the people who manage and use those materials that matter. Who owns it and how it is used is important. If it can be used for the benefit of humanity with God at the center and for good purposes, God will gladly grant ownership to that person.

Let us consider the types of properties we own. One of them is the former New Yorker Hotel building located at 34th Street and 8th Avenue in New York. When we purchased it, this massive hotel with 2,000 rooms was standing in the heart of Manhattan like a ruin. I doubted my eyes when I first saw the interior. It was like a wreck. It looked as if it had been bombed. It was reminiscent of Seoul right after the Korean War. I could not understand how such a ruin could be located in the middle of New York.

We purchased that building and transformed it into a vibrant place, and it is currently used as the World Mission Headquarters. It is like bringing the dead back to life to do God's work. The New Yorker Hotel is representative of the real estate we have acquired.

We are purchasing properties that have been abandoned and lifeless and making them maximally useful for God and humanity. Recently, we purchased the Columbia University Alumni Association building, which had been abandoned like a ruin, and after thorough repairs, it is now used as the headquarters of the American church. We also bought the Manhattan Center. This building was once the premier opera house in New York, but its beautiful appearance had long been lost and it had been in decline for decades. Our young members are currently repairing it for several months. It will also become a major sanctuary for our church.

Recently, we acquired the old Tiffany building to use as the headquarters of the 'News World' newspaper. It is well known that this building was once a symbol of America's prosperity and wealth. We also bought an old loft candy factory to use as the church's publishing department. Additionally, we purchased the Christian Brothers Seminary, which had been vacant for five years, along with 270 acres of land to establish a Unification seminary. We bought hundreds of acres of land in Barrytown, New York City, to use as the site for a future university.

We have invested a significant amount of church finances to acquire these properties. Who is this for? Of course, it is for our church members and their descendants, but ultimately it is for the general public. We have prepared these for the service of God and humanity. I believe that New York City will welcome our renovation projects simply for beautifying the city and improving the neighborhood's environment. What we are doing is truly innovative, and when the American people sincerely understand this, they will welcome it.

Our movement possesses the vitality, energy, and determination to revive the pioneering spirit of America. We are not only striving to restore the declining Christian spirit and the founding spirit of this nation but are also actively transforming lifeless buildings and desolate lands into productive and paradisiacal places.

8th Avenue in New York could rightly be called a street of prostitutes. We aim to transform it into a street filled with vitality and beauty. Our goal is to restore both spirit and body. As you may know, while conducting the Yankee Stadium campaign, we also launched the 'Beautification Movement of America.' Thousands of young members cleaned the dirty streets of New York City every morning. We hope this expands nationwide. The entire nation should participate in this movement. The American people should take pride in the beautiful land and environment that God has blessed them with.

The newspapers have incorrectly reported that I am becoming wealthy. While I have not directly said so, they imply that I have deposited a large sum of money in a Swiss bank. However, the members of the Unification Church who are with me know better. Personally, I own nothing. Everything is under the church's jurisdiction and is being managed and used appropriately for the purpose of building God's nation on earth.

Many people are skeptical about the source of our finances. Some believe that this money comes from the Korean Central Intelligence Agency or the Korean government or some other place. However, this funding is the result of the efforts of Unification Church members. It is the result of their blood and sweat and comes from sacrificial work. Our church members find it absurd when people who do not know the Unification Church say they are becoming robots and are being manipulated by someone. They know better than anyone why they are doing this and what it is for.

It is my hope and purpose to leave something behind in America. I will not live here permanently. Many people in the world come to America to gain something. I am the only one who has come here to give everything I have to America. Yet, I am receiving much criticism.

Question: The church's involvement in political matters is also a major controversy. What are your thoughts on the relationship between the church and politics or the world government?

Our movement is fundamentally spiritual and religious. However, our goal is not only to change the spiritual but also the physical. And this is aimed at all humanity.

How do we intend to accomplish this? It is not through violence or military coups but through education, especially the education of national leaders. This is where the Unification Church and I are involved. We testify to God not only to the countless people on the streets but also to the leaders who can guide the nation towards God. Our hope is to give them new life in their hearts so that they become God-centered leaders. This is how we aim to transform the world.

I do not think about seizing power in a nation or taking over the government. I have no ambition to become a senator in the United States or a governor of any state. My responsibility as a messenger of God is to convey God's word and will to those who have influence over the nation and society.

During the Watergate incident, people said, "The Unification Church is a political organization. They support Nixon. Their movement is political." Nevertheless, what do you think we actually did? We organized a 'Fasting Prayer Meeting to Overcome the National Emergency' and engaged in much prayer and fasting. Many members of the Unification Church fasted for three days or a week for the nation. We prayed overnight on the steps of the Capitol. We prayed for congressmen and the president in front of the White House and Lincoln Memorial. I remember that I appealed to the nation to pray for repentance and to seek mercy and forgiveness for national crimes during the state of emergency.

I viewed the Watergate incident as a national emergency. It was a moral crisis and a national crime. While American soldiers were dying in Vietnam, those at home were deeply wounded internally and were divided. They were losing faith in everything and could not send support for the war happening overseas. I believed that the only way to heal this was through God's grace and that the power of prayer could bring it about. I wanted this nation to offer prayers of repentance before God. I wanted to issue a declaration calling for prayer for the nation, just as President Lincoln had done. Our church wanted to set an example. I wanted the conscience of America to awaken. Is this a political activity?

If you read my statement regarding the Watergate incident, you would understand that the message of 'Forgive, Love, and Unite' was filled with the same spirit as the Sermon on the Mount. These three phrases express the essence of Christ's teachings and are far removed from political ambition.

Question: I would like to know about your prayer life. The prayer life of the Unification Church is considered unique, and many members say they can learn to pray in the church.

I believe prayer is the most powerful thing. It can turn the impossible into the possible. In the Unification Church, we emphasize prayer, but we do not pray in any special way; rather, the content is different. "Do not pray for yourself." This is my teaching. I teach that one should pray for their mission, for others, and that their prayers should ascend to God as words of comfort.

Question: I see that the doctrine of True Parents has caused many misunderstandings. Please explain the relationship between True Parents and physical parents, as well as the duties that children should take towards them.

The term "parents" refers to the father and mother who gave life to oneself. Our concept of True Parents is related to the rebirth of an individual.

The essence of humanity is spiritual. Our essence is intangible, and it is in a fallen state of death. Therefore, all humans are destined to be reborn by God.

Ultimately, because God is spiritual and intangible, humans cannot receive teachings and experiences of rebirth directly from God. Thus, God has established central figures so that humans can receive teachings and experience rebirth through them. These figures are the tangible and intangible True Parents. This concept of True Parents is entirely different from that of physical parents and does not belittle physical parents.

After the fall of Adam and Eve, God has been reconstructing the family. Since the human family originated from fallen Adam and Eve, God cannot accept it as it is. It must go through a process of re-creation and rebirth. This is the teaching of Jesus Christ 2,000 years ago. Therefore, we need God and the True Parents appointed by God.

Physical parents give their children physical life and love and raise them with the best moral principles they can. However, True Parents give spiritual life. The term "Holy Father" has long been used in the church to refer to God. Therefore, the term "True Parents" is not so unfamiliar.

Adam and Eve were destined to become the True Parents of humanity in God's plan. However, when they fell, God appointed Jesus as the True Parent of humanity. When he was crucified, God promised another Messiah. He comes to realize the ideal of True Parents centered on God. He will give birth to a new family of God according to God's ideal. When we have True Parents centered on God, we will all become true brothers and sisters.

Question: After being spiritually reborn, what is the relationship and duty of children towards their physical parents?

His bloodline parents will clearly remain his parents, and the family relationship will never change eternally. However, after spiritual rebirth, he is connected to God's family and has the responsibility to restore his physical parents, siblings, and relatives to God's family. Doing so is the way to establish an eternal relationship with those he loves before God.

The relationship with the True Family is eternal, while the relationship with the secular family becomes temporary. Therefore, they must lead their physically related family members differently before God. The ultimate goal that humanity must achieve on earth is to become God's true sons and daughters. Park Bo-hee: Yes. The strength given by God and ginseng currently guarantees health doubly.
