Q: As the church grows and expands, becoming increasingly successful, and as the pioneering era passes, do you foresee any problems in maintaining your pioneering spirit?  
Our pioneering spirit will continue to remain vibrant and alive. Until God's purpose is fulfilled, no one can rest or relax. Becoming a Christian is not our only goal.  
My goal is to save this world, but that is not the end of it. We must liberate God and the entire spirit world. The Unification Church is the first church to explain that God is in pain. In this regard, our goal is complete liberation, that is, to free God from sorrow.  
Partial success is not complete success. Our goal is so high that it cannot be easily reached or easily satisfied. I often ask my congregation, "As you know, I have worked hard for over 30 years, shouldn't I retire and enjoy some rest?" However, I have never entertained such thoughts in my heart. Because I am always at the forefront of the pioneering movement to achieve our goals.  
In fact, I have never reproached those who call us a cult. Our way of life is so innovative that it appears heretical in their eyes. We aim to liberate God. And we aim to liberate Jesus Christ. We seek to free them from sorrow and heart-wrenching pain. Has anyone ever said such things throughout history? We are not just speaking; we are living it.  
My desire to serve God is truly revolutionary. God knows how to laugh, but more importantly, He knows how to feel sorrow and pain. When He looks at suffering humanity, He has the heart of a parent whose heart is torn apart. Like any parent, God wants to stop the suffering of His children. He wants to give happiness to His children.  
They say Jesus Christ is in glory at the right hand of God. However, I say this: "Let us not only liberate this world from sin but also liberate God and Jesus from pain and sorrow." Do you think Jesus would say, "God, Reverend Moon is wrong. Cast him out. We do not need his help. He is a blasphemer. I am the way, the truth, and the life, and no one can come to you except through me"? Would Jesus criticize me like this for trying to fulfill my mission?  
No. Jesus would say, "God, bless him. His mission must be fulfilled. The fulfillment of his mission is the fulfillment of my mission. Therefore, his success is my success and God's success. God, help him. Inspire him to achieve the best success he can in his lifetime."  
The concept of condemnation in Christianity is fundamentally wrong. Because God is the center of love, He does not condemn anyone. However, people reap what they sow. Those who sow bad seeds on earth go to hell after death. But that is not a result of God's condemnation. Those who live and act contrary to God's will cannot enter heaven. Because God is the center of love, when He sees humanity suffering in hell, He feels a pain that tears His heart apart. Moreover, He cannot find joy in seeing that. God's ultimate hope is to liberate even hell.  
In this physical world, we can leave great achievements and advance through our activities. This earthly life is a once-in-a-lifetime opportunity. This is the opportunity to build a foundation for eternal life. Let’s say one lives for a hundred years on earth. A hundred years on earth is shorter than a fleeting moment compared to eternity. We must willingly invest this hundred years for God and humanity.  
Do not live for yourself even for a moment. If you dedicate your life to God without selfish desires, you will enjoy a more valuable happiness, and God will reward you with eternal life in heaven.  
Q: After Reverend Moon passes away, what problems do you think the church and this movement will face? How do you think Unification Church members will cope when Reverend Moon is no longer here?  
I have fulfilled my personal mission on this earth. Therefore, it makes no difference whether I am here or in the spirit world. Our movement has laid a solid foundation. What remains is only the human position on earth; spiritually, it has already been achieved. Because its root is in God and the spirit world. Based on this foundation, our movement will never fail. It will continue even in my absence and will truly establish God's kingdom on earth.  
Q: What risks do you foresee as the Unification Church becomes institutionalized like other churches? Will senior members take control and try to dominate?  
That is fundamentally what distinguishes the established churches from the Unification Church. Our movement seeks to unify, not to become a single denomination. Therefore, this movement will continue with revolutionary zeal and pioneering spirit until God's kingdom is established on this earth. In other words, it will never cease until God can escape the pain He has endured for 6,000 years of history (according to the Bible) and enjoy joy and rest.  
We do not simply want to become an institutionally established church. That is our true nature, and we will not rest until this movement is no longer needed.  
Q: Do you feel that the plans you have set are at a successful stage? Or do you think adjustments need to be made to future plans? Have your plans gone as intended so far?  
Our basic plan does not change. And the goals we set have been achieved every time. I believe we have achieved all the goals we planned up to now.  
My visit to America was certainly planned, and the following three and a half years of work were also planned. The Yankee Stadium event, of course, and the Washington Monument event were planned, and the current nationwide tour of lectures in the U.S. for 1977-78 is also scheduled.  
Q: I understand that the "Divine Principle" was initially transmitted orally. The early believers told me that they heard the principles in the form of sermons, and that it was only during the Busan period that the principles were finally written down. The current "Principle of Education" is very detailed and organized compared to the early version. Do you see any need for changes, refinements, additions, or deletions in the current "Principle of Education"? Is this form finalized?  
Many new attempts will be made in the partial expressions of the Divine Principle. However, the fundamental content of the revelation from beginning to end will not change at all. For example, the central ideas seen in "Creation Principles," "The Fall," and "The Purpose of the Messiah's Advent and His Second Coming" will never change. However, I understand that there are difficulties in expressing certain concepts or ideas of our philosophy. Therefore, one of my major tasks, which will take considerable time and effort, is to refine the "Principle of Education" once again and present it before history. This task remains to be completed.  
The "Divine Principle" cannot be changed simply because it is discussed or because people do not like it. Such a thing can never happen. Moreover, there are still many truths that have not yet been announced. I have already received such revelations but am intentionally withholding them for future announcement.  
Q: Do you believe that you still have future revelations to clarify?  
The Divine Principle is not a philosophy or a doctrine; it is, like the very word itself, God's Principle (Divine Principle). This is God's unchanging truth. Once that truth is revealed, we must live according to that principle and act under that principle. At the very least, a foundation must be laid for the fulfillment of that principle. Then Satan cannot invade.  
When a person becomes completely one with the truth, Satan cannot take him away from God. For example, if God and Adam and Eve had been completely united around the truth, there would have been no room for Satan to invade.  
Truth must be actualized. Truth must exist and be fulfilled in living human beings. Otherwise, truth can be taken away and misused by Satan. That is why I do not reveal new truths until all conditions are met and truth is substantively realized to a certain extent.  
Furthermore, in some respects, the Divine Principle is also a record of my life. It is my own life experience. This Divine Principle is within me, and I am within the Divine Principle.  
Q: People outside the Unification Church think that all members worship Reverend Moon as an individual, but when I asked Unification Church members about this, they stated that their loyalty is based on the Divine Principle. Do you agree that people's loyalty is to the principle? Since you are the one who revealed, announced, and is the source of the principle, is it accurate to say that you are connected to the principle?  
That question is very important. Many people say that I am merely the announcer and transmitter of the truth, but I live according to the truth and have actualized it. Therefore, the only way for people to understand me and my actions is through the principle. They can only understand me by knowing and studying the Divine Principle. This is also why our members can understand me better and be more loyal to me the more they study the principle. The two are one and the same. However, even within our church, no one understands God one hundred percent.  
Q: Reverend Moon, you are often criticized as authoritarian, even dictatorial, and military-like. What is your personal definition of authority, and how do you express it? How do you express your personal authority in relation to church members?  
In fact, those who understand the Divine Principle well do not think that way. Authority is merely an appearance. People take a glance and then say I am authoritarian.  
Let’s think about God. Then one could also say that God is a dictator. He has no council to report to, nor was He elected. However, no one calls God a dictator. It is because He is the source of love.  
Love is stronger than any authority. Therefore, when people see only my authority, they regard me as a dictator. But they completely miss the point. I am in the position of a father to my members. Parents love their children, not dominate them. If we were to remove the spiritual characteristic of love, that is, God's love, from the Unification Church, it would not exist.  
Q: Why do many people and the media overlook the spiritual aspect of the Unification Church and your spiritual nature?  
I believe it is because they deliberately refuse to see that aspect. That is precisely what is important. They seem to have already drawn their conclusions and are only trying to find evidence to support those conclusions.  
However, those who know us closely see that there is infinite unity and warm friendship and love in our church, which originates from God and radiates through me.  
We have always faced attacks but have always triumphed and succeeded. Even while being hit, we gain, and the "Principle" is amazing. In 1976, the whole world took a stance against me. There was controversy about us in every country. Rather, I sent missionaries to 120 countries to further promote it. This allowed them to serve as lightning rods attracting global persecution. The greater the persecution, the faster the satanic world loses its power. This is a heavenly strategy.  
Who would know this strategy? However, there will come a time when people truly understand the Unification Church and me. The truth will be revealed, and the message of love will be taught. On that day, their regrets will be great.  
Q: You have spoken about the way you have been attacked so far. You say you do not retaliate, but interestingly, outsiders are saying the opposite. They fear that as the Unification Church grows in power, Reverend Moon will command the members to take up arms and go out like an army. What do you think about people's thoughts that you would use violence or force to achieve your goals?  
God's principle never attacks first. Demons and Satan always try to attack and destroy the opponent first. However, on the heavenly side, there is a responsibility to defend oneself. I teach that our movement is fundamentally non-violent and non-military. We have the greatest weapon, which is truth. We also have a great goal: that human hearts reach God's heart.  
Truth can change hearts. When a person's heart, which is the motive for his actions, changes, all actions and plans change. This is the basic method by which we influence the world of evil with the words given by God. We are conquerors by love and truth, not by violence or weapons.  
Now, at a time when the threat of a third world war looms everywhere in the world, whether there will be a war or not depends on human responsibility.  
Even if we exclude the possibility of war, we can see that there are hostile camps in the world. The communist camp representing Satan and the democratic camp representing God are in confrontation. Communists seek to conquer this world by violence, but God desires to possess this world by love. We must become the embodiment of love that fulfills God's will.  
Q: The media frequently criticize that members of the Unification Church deceive others in economic activities as if they are not Unification Church members and that the church uses front organizations. Will the church tolerate this, and what reason is there to hide the church's activities?  
I teach honesty, purity, and sacrifice from a principled standpoint. First of all, humans must be honest before God. The Divine Principle teaches that human deceit brings separation between God and humans. Even if our members face harsher persecution, I must serve them as God's envoy and emphasize that they should first reveal themselves as Unification Church members to others.  
Unification Church members are members of the Unification Church and follow Reverend Moon.
and restore the spirit of Christianity that is fading away. I believe that the revival of the Christian spirit in America is essential for the fulfillment of its divine mission.

My ultimate hope is to see this nation truly come before God. When a nation stands before God, it becomes the motivation for the entire world to become one. Although America is treating me arbitrarily due to ignorance and misunderstanding, I have no hostility in my heart. I know why this phenomenon is occurring, and I see it as part of God's plan. Because of this, whether positively or negatively, I have quickly become a famous person in American society. At the very least, I have been able to attract America's attention. Soon, the American people will come to know the new revelation that is God's truth. 

What I feared the most was American indifference towards me. However, Americans have not been indifferent. Now I can show the truth to Americans. 

My mission is cosmic. My concern is for all humanity in this world and the next. My mission encompasses the past, present, and future, and includes all of humanity.

This is why I must travel around the world preaching, and it is also the reason for sending missionaries of the Unification Church worldwide. This is God's strategy, but no one understands it. Some even say I am a madman. 

We Unification Church members have responded to God's call and volunteered to dedicate ourselves to the cosmic movement of restoring heaven. The world is now in a fortunate time. Today's America is a microcosm of the world. The fate of America will influence the fate of the world and God's providence. God has a definite plan that He wants to unfold in this country. I said at the Yankee Stadium gathering, “If a disease occurs in your family, would you not need to bring in a doctor from outside? If there is a fire in your house, would you not need to bring in a firefighter from outside? God has entrusted me with the responsibility of being a doctor and a firefighter and has sent me to America.” 

At the Washington Monument rally on September 18, 1976, I also declared, “God has sent me to deliver a new revelation to this country. And He has specifically called me to guide the young people who will be the future leaders of America to Him.” 

I have never heard any American religious leader make such a bold proclamation. How can someone from Korea say such things? I am not speaking for myself, nor am I seeking my own glory. I know who God is and what He wants to command, so every word I speak is truly prophetic. 

While some may not understand, I must speak. I am Korean, but from God's perspective, I am the best American who can truly reveal the essence of the American spirit more than any American. When this spirit spreads in this land, America will prosper and thrive. 

Imagine if God suddenly appeared here in America. What would He say? Would He say, “You are doing well; I am satisfied. Keep doing this”? The answer is “No.” It is clear that people's hearts are filled with spiritual and moral struggles, and if the current state is left unchanged, America cannot escape divine punishment. We know this. 

Before it is too late, someone must convey God's will. I have come to America with warnings and declarations. Many people may laugh at my words, but history will never laugh at me. This is because it is not my words, but God's words being spoken through me. 

For earthly beings, the spiritual world is a labyrinth. The path to that world is indeed a maze. It is impossible for humans to find the exact passage to the spiritual world on their own. You cannot discover your destination without finding a leader to guide you, and unless someone paves the way. Unification Church members are the luckiest people because they have a spiritual light to guide their path. 

Do you know that there is a spiritual world? “Yes.” Raise your hand if you know it, those who know it. And among you, those who have experienced it rather than just knowing it. (Many hands go up) Wow! (Laughter) 

The reason humans turn away from religion is that you are quite curious about the spiritual world. There are countless religions in the world today, and those religions seek to establish a relationship with the spiritual world, the world of eternal life, the world of living with God. That world is the destination of religion, and you have a general idea of that. 

However, now religion has become increasingly marginalized, concluding that “Religion is for the weak. It is unnecessary for us humans. It is merely a moral representation manipulated by humans.” 

Even just looking at Christianity, which is the center of religion... America is the representative country of the Christian nations worldwide, and you, who grew up in American families, are those who once believed in Christianity but have turned away from religion and have been living as you please, and now, having nowhere to go, have come back here again. (Laughter) 

You might be going around in circles here and might go out again! “No.” There are not many saying “No.” (Laughter) 

So why did you, who believed in Christianity, which is centered around God, the center of the world and all ideals, come out of it? 

The first reason is that you did not truly know that there is a spiritual world. Humans have the ability to compare, and because they have the intelligence to compare, when there is a good place, they will leave the bad and go there, and when there is a higher and more valuable place, they will go there. That is human nature. Is that right? “Yes.” It is probably more so for women than for men. (Laughter) Men are the same, right? “Yes.” It is all the same. The next reason is that you did not know God. 

The third reason is that you did not know that love, which is the center of the spiritual world and the center of God, is what binds everything together. You did not know these three things. Even if you know God and the spiritual world, you only know that it is dry and that it is no different from the human world, and you only feel uncomfortable being under the absolute God. You did not know that there is a world centered on love. 

The fundamental reason for the unity of spirit and body is God's love. 

Now, where there is love, the logic that it is okay to go up, down, or be in the middle holds true. Does a loving husband dislike his wife just because she is lower than him, or does a loving wife hate her husband just because he is higher than her? They are one, one. When they become one, they can freely go from low to high and from high to low, or be in the middle, and can go anywhere. There are no restrictions here. Is that right? “Yes.” 

In today's world, many say, “This world must be one. It must be a world of unity. It must be a world of peace.” 

So, will we create unity by forcing it with strength, shouting “Yah!” or will we create it with some organizational power? Nowadays, it is a society of organizations, so will we make unity with strong organizational power? Then, what ideology will we use to create unity? There may be some possibility for that, but it cannot be done with our nature, where both body and mind are completely in harmony and say, “This must be it.” That is absolutely impossible. Body and mind cannot say, “This is good. This is what I desire. This is the eternal ideal that I can serve and live by.” That cannot be done with money, knowledge, or anything else. 

So, what is the fundamental thing that can unite everyone, whether they are high or low, from east or west, yellow, white, or black? It is love. You must understand that there is no other conclusion than that true love is what unites us. 

Do you think so? “Yes.” What can my body and mind become close and united with? Can they be pleased by money? That cannot last forever. 

The conclusion is that all five senses must come together and unite to laugh and dance in the ideal realm of true love. Who can deny that? If you deny it, you are not human. Therefore, the conclusion is that the spirit and body, our mind and body, can all unite and resonate together only in the realm of true love. 

Difference between mind and spirit 

The spiritual world and the physical world, spiritual beings and physical beings are the same. Here, God's love is centered, and God is at the center. The fallen human beings we usually think of are not centered on God. Humans are made of mind and body, but that is different. That is a different dimension. Mind and spirit are different. The spiritual world and the physical world are discussed in relation to God's love. Therefore, for the spiritual world and the physical world to unite, God must be involved. Without God's love, there is no spiritual world. The spiritual world is connected through God. 

Do you have a conscience? How is the conscience different from the spiritual world? You have a mind and body, right? How is the mind different from the spiritual world? What is the difference? “My mind is also spirit, right?” You are thinking like that. You are confused. You must understand clearly. The mind is not the spiritual world. Because it is fallen, the mind does not relate to the spiritual world. In other words, the mind of fallen humans is like that of a person without bones. If you think of the mind of fallen humans as like a person without bones, it becomes more real. The mind of fallen humans is like the form of a person without bones. 

When you look at the spiritual body, it also has a body and a mind. The spiritual body has a mind and a body, and the mind of the spiritual body is like the spiritual world. It must be related to God. Therefore, without a relationship with God, nothing like the mind of the spiritual body can arise. Do you understand what I am saying? You must recognize that spirit and mind are different. The mind is unrelated to God. In other words, it has departed from God. God cannot relate to it. God cannot directly govern it. 

That is why your minds change back and forth, right? Is that true or not? “It is.” Even communists think that because their consciousness and minds change, their consciousness revolution can easily change. They think that religion and everything else do not exist. However, the spiritual world, spiritual relationships, and spiritual beings do not change. They steadily pursue one eternal goal. Why is that? Because they stand on God's side. Do you understand what I am saying? The mind belongs to humanity. It belongs to the fluctuating human nature. 

You have learned the principle and understand what the original mind is, right? The original mind is an existence that moves toward a new purpose, combining the mind and spirit, and can create the ideal self centered on God, united with our conscience. That is how you can see it. Do you understand what I am saying? Therefore, without the original mind, you cannot find, discover, or establish the source of your relationship with the spiritual world, ideals, true love, and everything else. That is the conclusion. 

When the original mind arises within me, my body also becomes happy, and everything follows it. This automatically leads to unity. It begins to unite.
Do you understand what that means? Huh? The biggest problem for humanity so far has been that the body and mind are separated from each other. You all agree, right? "Yes." However, when the spiritual realm, or spiritual power, comes upon me and I can have a sincere desire, then the mind and body naturally become one. A revolution occurs from that foundation, and as long as we cannot discover the source that corrects the foundation, we have no way to seek ideals. There must be a motive for a result to come about. Does that sound right to you?

What is religion? It is to implant the divine mind within us. This divine mind is a core element, and there are numerous religions centered around it. There are various forms of religion, and all kinds of shapes exist. Some are like this... (pointing while speaking) But this divine mind does not just connect automatically. It has been spinning around, but it does not connect. If there is a divine mind here, then it goes like this, but it cannot reach here and goes around like this... We are playing such games. (pointing while speaking)

Originally, if you find your way in, when this reaches here, it automatically connects and comes back out. It does not take a different path but returns to the same path. Now, in the Unification Church, when choosing a husband or wife, will you marry someone who is smooth and has a degree from a university or graduate school, or will you marry someone who has thrown away all schooling and is just wandering around trying to save the world, someone whose face is dark and looks terrible? "The latter." Why, why? Because the carat of gold, whether it is 14-karat or 8-karat, is high... Do you understand now? "Yes."

What kind of gold has a high purity? A handsome man, a very good-looking man, but will you marry a man who is just a bum, or will you marry a man who looks terrible, like a ghost from the Unification Church, or a black man? "A black man." Will you marry an ugly black man? "Yes." (Laughter) The view of marriage is different. The Unification Church's view of marriage is different.

What is different in the Unification Church? The view of marriage is different. Also, the view of love is different, the view of love. Do you understand? It is to become a lump of pure gold rather than a pure gold hammer, to love once like lightning, as the universe desires. Women will give birth to children, and in their virginity, they will offer their milk, which they used to hide from others—though in America, they do not do that anymore—to their babies, feeling the thunder of love and the shaking of heaven and earth, and feeling that God is laughing heartily. Are you confident? (Laughter)

While looking at the baby, can you say, "My husband is so precious that I cannot exchange him for heaven and earth, and because my husband is better than God, this son is a son who can receive God's love"? Can you say that? "Yes." Why? Why can you say that? Because you see through the eyes of God's love. In love, there is nothing ugly. If you love someone, you even like the dirty toes of your wife. (Laughter) Even something dirty is beautiful. It is good. (Laughter) Married people know that. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

No matter how ugly your husband is, if you see him with love, he is like God, and no matter how unpleasant he seems, he is a precious husband whom you cannot exchange for heaven and earth.

That is why you should not worry about being good-looking or not. The question is whether you can be a husband or wife who can possess God's love. Do you understand what that means? You must become such people and form families that live in God's love.

Now, I did not finish talking today. I will have to continue next time. Today, since time has passed a lot... (Applause) Next Sunday, we might meet at three o'clock. Is that okay? "Yes." (Applause) At that time, no one will be absent. No one will be absent. (Laughter)

So, understand that today, it is only about "We must become such brides and grooms." That is all I wanted you to know. Next time, if the teacher speaks about something else, please remind me, "Oh, teacher, you said you would continue that story." "Yes."
